<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kontrakt</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kontrakt</i>, from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">contractus</i>.

***контролировавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:контролировавший.html>контроли́ровавший</a> (4958)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***контролировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:контролировать.html>контроли́ровать</a> (4958)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контролировать.html>контроли́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kontrolírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проконтроли́ровать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to control, to check</li>
<li>to monitor, to supervise</li>
<li>to rule, to superintend (<i>no perfective form</i>)</li></ol>

***контроль.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:контроль.html>контро́ль</a> (1916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">contrôle</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контроль.html>контро́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kontrólʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контроль.html>контро́ля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контроль.html>контро́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контроль.html>контро́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>control</li>
<li>checkup, checking, inspection, monitoring, supervision, verification</li>
<li>blank test, standard</li>
<li>institution or organization that carries out such checks, inspections or monitoring</li>
<li>area at the entrance to a theater where tickets are checked or collected</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ticket-collectors, inspectors</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контроль.html>контро́ль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kontrólʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контрольный.html>контро́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kontrólʹnyj</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контузия.html>конту́зия</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kontúzija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контузить.html>конту́зить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kontúzitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bruise, to contuse

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:контузия.html>конту́зия</a> (17441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контузия.html>конту́зия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kontúzija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контузия.html>конту́зии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контузия.html>конту́зии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контузия.html>конту́зий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>contusion</li>
<li>shell shock</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:контур.html>ко́нтур</a> (7815)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контур.html>ко́нтур</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kóntur</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контур.html>ко́нтура</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контур.html>ко́нтуры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контур.html>ко́нтуров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>contour, outline</li>
<li>circuit</li></ol>

***конфисковать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конфисковать.html>конфискова́ть</a> (14329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">confiscāre</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конфисковать.html>конфискова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konfiskovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to confiscate, to seize</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конфликтный.html>конфли́ктный</a> (17542)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конфликт.html>конфли́кт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konflíkt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конфликтный.html>конфли́ктный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konflíktnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> conflict
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:конфликтный.html>конфли́ктная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:комиссия.html>коми́ссия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>konflíktnaja</b> komíssija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">arbitration tribunal; grievance committee</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>contentious, quarrelsome, disputatious
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:конфликтный.html>конфли́ктное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>konflíktnoje</b> délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">disputed matter/case</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***конфликтовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конфликтовать.html>конфликтова́ть</a> (27847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конфликт.html>конфли́кт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konflíkt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конфликтовать.html>конфликтова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konfliktovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to conflict <i>(with)</i>, to clash <i>(with)</i>, to come up <i>(against)</i></li></ol>

***конфронтация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конфронтация.html>конфронта́ция</a> (22166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конфронтация.html>конфронта́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konfrontácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конфронтация.html>конфронта́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конфронтация.html>конфронта́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конфронтация.html>конфронта́ций</a></b>)
